{"nick":"joepie91","message":"Pistos: btw, the specific risks with process.exit are that 1) because your script can be doing multiple things simultaneously, calling process.exit in the wrong place can interrupt some task that's still ongoing, and 2) even when nothing seems to be ongoing anymore, it's possible that whatever is keeping the process alive still needs to be shut down cleanly to make sure all necessary data is written to disk, etc. -- both of these can cause data","date":"2018-01-24T12:39:54.995Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"corruption if they occur and you don't handle them properly","date":"2018-01-24T12:39:56.491Z","type":"message"}
